**Stock Market Analysis Report**------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Last Closing Candle**

The last closing candle in the provided 90 days of price data is for the trading day of **2024-07-08**. The open price for this candle was **166.5399932861328**, the high was **167.72000122070312**, the low was **165.6199951171875**, and the close was **166.52000427246094**.

**Volume**

The volume for this candle was **3,499,800**.

**Moving Averages**

The 50-day simple moving average (SMA) is **164.59219909667968**, and the 200-day SMA is **154.99970001220703**. The price is currently above the 50-day SMA but below the 200-day SMA, which could suggest a period of consolidation or a potential trend change.

The exponential moving averages (EMAs) for 50 and 200 days are **164.61779907226563** and **155.16255004882814**, respectively. The 50-day EMA is above the 200-day EMA, a bullish signal known as the "golden cross," which could suggest that the stock may be starting to trend upwards.

**Momentum Indicators**

The relative strength index (RSI) for the last candle is **37.3123327651187**. An RSI below 30 typically indicates that a stock is oversold, while an RSI above 70 suggests that it is overbought. A value of 37.31 is relatively neutral.

The moving average convergence divergence (MACD) for the last candle is **-1.3234709365405877**. A negative MACD value suggests that the short-term EMA is below the long-term EMA, which could indicate a bearish trend.

**Volatility Indicators**

The Bollinger Bands for the last candle are **(9.580892493065667, 17.921424234045176, 15.22328744608051)** for the upper, middle, and lower bands, respectively. The close price is near the lower Bollinger Band, which could suggest that the stock is oversold and due for a rebound.

The average true range (ATR) for the last candle is **1.7921424234045176**. A higher ATR value indicates greater volatility, while a lower ATR value suggests lower volatility.

**Conclusion**

Based on this analysis, the last closing candle does not necessarily indicate a clear bullish or bearish trend. The stock price has been range-bound for the past few days, and the indicators are relatively neutral. However, the fact that the close price is near the lower Bollinger Band and the 50-day EMA is above the 200-day EMA could suggest that the stock may be due for a rebound in the near term. As always, traders and investors should consider multiple factors and indicators when making investment decisions.

2024-07-12bullish
**Stock Market Report (2024-07-12)**

**Bullish Engulfing Pattern Identified**

The last closing candle exhibited a bullish engulfing pattern, which is generally considered a bullish signal. This pattern is characterized by a small bearish candle followed by a large bullish candle, where the body of the bullish candle completely engulfs the body of the bearish candle.

**Key Characteristics of the Last Closing Candle**

| Metric | Value |
|------------------|-----------------------|
| Open | 299.59 |
| Close | 310.63 |
| High | 312.02 |
| Low | 299.03 |
| Body size | 11.04 |
| Upper wick | 0.99 |
| Lower wick | 1.40 |
| Previous candle | Bearish |
| Body size (prev) | 0.51 |
| Upper wick (prev) | 0.00 |
| Lower wick (prev) | 0.51 |

**Analysis**

The last closing candle displayed a large body size of 11.04, indicating strong buying pressure. The upper wick of 0.99 and lower wick of 1.40 suggest that the market tested both resistance and support levels during the period but ultimately closed near the high of the day.

The bullish engulfing pattern is often interpreted as a sign of a potential trend reversal. This pattern suggests that the bulls have taken control of the market and that the price may continue to rise.

However, it is essential to note that technical analysis should not be used in isolation and should be complemented with other forms of analysis, such as fundamental analysis. While the last closing candle is a bullish signal, it does not guarantee that the price will continue to rise. Therefore, it is crucial to exercise caution and consider other factors before making any investment decisions.
